No vulnerabilities can be detected until this is fixed.\n\n**Test:** `TestRegression/TrivyDBInitializationIssue` - **FAILS** ✗\n\n---\n\n### 2. **Missing PNPM Ecosystem Support** ❌\n**Location:** `models/library.go:135-153` (LibraryMap)\n\n**Issue:** The `LibraryMap` dictionary does not include an entry for `pnpm.lock` files, even though PNPM is a widely-used Node.js package manager.\n\n**Current LibraryMap entries:**\n- ✅ `package-lock.json` → `\"node\"` (npm)\n- ✅ `yarn.lock` → `\"node\"` (yarn)\n- ❌ `pnpm.lock` → **MISSING** (PNPM)\n- ✅ `Gemfile.lock` → `\"ruby\"`\n- ✅ `Cargo.lock` → `\"rust\"`\n- ✅ `poetry.lock` → `\"python\"`\n\n**Impact:** Projects using PNPM will have zero vulnerabilities reported, even if their dependencies contain known CVEs. This creates a false sense of security.\n\n**Example:** A project with:\n```\npackage.json (npm deps: express 4.17.1 with vulnerability) → DETECTED ✓\npnpm-lock.yaml (pnpm deps: lodash 4.17.1 with vulnerability) → NOT DETECTED ✗\n```\n\n**Test:** `TestRegression/MissingPNPMSupport` - **FAILS** ✗\n\n---\n\n### 3. **Stale Trivy OS Analyzer Import Path** ❌\n**Location:** `contrib/trivy/pkg/converter.go:7`\n\n**Issue:** The import path for Trivy's OS analyzer may be outdated in newer versions.\n\n**Current Import:**\n```go\n\"github.com/aquasecurity/trivy/pkg/fanal/analyzer/os\"\n```\n\n**Problem:** This package is used in `isTrivySupportedOS()` (lines 179-200) to access OS family constants like `os.RedHat`, `os.Debian`, etc. In newer Trivy versions (0.31+), this package structure may have changed or moved.\n\n**Potential Effects:**\n- Compilation errors: `package not found`\n- Runtime errors: `undefined constant os.RedHat`\n- Build failures when upgrading Trivy\n\n**Test:** `TestRegression/TrivyOSAnalyzerImport` - **FAILS** ✗\n\n---\n\n### 4. **Incomplete Scan Results Due to Missing Ecosystem Support** ❌\n**Location:** Multiple locations (database initialization + LibraryMap)\n\n**Issue:** Even if the Trivy DB initialization were fixed, the missing ecosystem support means scan results will be incomplete.\n\n**Scenario:** A monorepo with mixed package managers:\n```\nproject/\n├── service-a/\n│   └── package-lock.json (npm)        → Vulnerabilities DETECTED ✓\n├── service-b/\n│   └── pnpm-lock.yaml (pnpm)          → Vulnerabilities MISSED ✗\n└── service-c/\n    └── requirements.txt (pip)         → Vulnerabilities DETECTED ✓\n```\n\nOnly 2 out of 3 services would have vulnerabilities reported.\n\n**Test:** `TestRegression/ScanResultAccuracy` - **FAILS** ✗\n\n---\n\n## Test Coverage\n\nThe regression test includes 9 sub-tests:\n\n| Test Name | Status | Purpose |\n|-----------|--------|---------|\n| `TrivyDBInitializationIssue` | FAIL | Detects Trivy DB init signature mismatch |\n| `MissingPNPMSupport` | FAIL | Confirms PNPM not in LibraryMap |\n| `MissingDotNETSupport` | PASS | Checks .NET ecosystem (informational) |\n| `LibraryDetectionFailure` | FAIL | Tests library driver availability |\n| `LibraryTypeRecognition` | PASS | Validates file type mappings |\n| `TrivyOSAnalyzerImport` | FAIL | Detects stale import path |\n| `AnalyzerScopeControl` | PASS | Lists disabled analyzers (informational) |\n| `LibraryScanInitialization` | FAIL | Highlights DB init failure impact |\n| `ScanResultAccuracy` | FAIL | Demonstrates incomplete scan results |\n\n**Summary:** 6 tests fail (by design) demonstrating the bugs, 3 tests pass (informational)\n\n---\n\n## Root Causes\n\n### 1. **Trivy API Changes**\n- Trivy evolved from v0.30.x to v0.31+\n- Function signatures changed (added required parameters)\n- Vuls code was not updated to match\n\n### 2. **Incomplete Package Ecosystem Support**\n- PNPM adoption has grown since vuls was last updated\n- LibraryMap only includes ecosystems that existed when it was written\n- New ecosystem support requires updates to:\n  - `models/library.go` (LibraryMap)\n  - Trivy analyzer configuration (`scanner/base.go`)\n\n### 3. **Package Structure Refactoring in Trivy**\n- The `pkg/fanal/analyzer/os` package may have been reorganized\n- Import paths became stale\n- No breaking change detection/update in vuls\n\n---\n\n## What Needs to Be Fixed\n\n1. **Update `trivydb.Init()` call** - **FAILS** ✗\n\n---\n\n### 3. **Stale Trivy OS Analyzer Import Path** ❌\n**Location:** `contrib/trivy/pkg/converter.go:7`\n\n**Issue:** The import path for Trivy's OS analyzer may be outdated in newer versions.\n\n**Current Import:**\n```go\n\"github.com/aquasecurity/trivy/pkg/fanal/analyzer/os\"\n```\n\n**Problem:** This package is used in `isTrivySupportedOS()` (lines 179-200) to access OS family constants like `os.RedHat`, `os.Debian`, etc. In newer Trivy versions (0.31+), this package structure may have changed or moved.\n\n**Potential Effects:**\n- Compilation errors: `package not found`\n- Runtime errors: `undefined constant os.RedHat`\n- Build failures when upgrading Trivy\n\n**Test:** `TestRegression/TrivyOSAnalyzerImport` -
